Istio’s powerful features provide a uniform and more efficient way to secure, connect, and monitor services. Istio is the path to load balancing, service-to-service authentication, and monitoring – with few or no service code changes.\\n18: \\n19: - For in-depth information about how to use Istio, visit [istio.io](https://istio.io)\\n20: - To ask questions and get assistance from our community, visit [GitHub Discussions](https://github.com/istio/istio/discussions)\\n21: - To learn how to participate in our overall community, visit [our community page](https://istio.io/about/community)\\n22: \\n23: In this README:\\n24: \\n25: - [Introduction](#introduction)\\n26: - [Repositories](#repositories)\\n27: - [Issue management](#issue-management)\\n28: \\n29: In addition, here are some other documents you may wish to read:\\n30: \\n31: - [Istio Community](https://github.com/istio/community#istio-community) - describes how to get involved and contribute to the Istio project\\n32: - [Istio Developer's Guide](https://github.com/istio/istio/wiki/Preparing-for-Development) - explains how to set up and use an Istio development environment\\n33: - [Project Conventions](https://github.com/istio/istio/wiki/Development-Conventions) - describes the conventions we use within the code base\\n34: - [Creating Fast and Lean Code](https://github.com/istio/istio/wiki/Writing-Fast-and-Lean-Code) - performance-oriented advice and guidelines for the code base\\n35: \\n36: You'll find many other useful documents on our [Wiki](https://github.com/istio/istio/wiki).\\n37: \\n38: ## Introduction\\n39: \\n40: [Istio](https://istio.io/latest/docs/concepts/what-is-istio/) is an open platform for providing a uniform way to [integrate\\n41: microservices](https://istio.io/latest/docs/examples/microservices-istio/), manage [traffic flow](https://istio.io/latest/docs/concepts/traffic-management/) across microservices, enforce policies\\n42: and aggregate telemetry data. Istio's control plane provides an abstraction\\n43: layer over the underlying cluster management platform, such as Kubernetes.\\n44: \\n45: Istio is composed of these components:\\n46: \\n47: - **Envoy** - Sidecar proxies per microservice to handle ingress/egress traffic\\n48:    between services in the cluster and from a service to external\\n49:    services. The proxies form a _secure microservice mesh_ providing a rich\\n50:    set of functions like discovery, rich layer-7 routing, circuit breakers,\\n51:    policy enforcement and telemetry recording/reporting\\n52:    functions.\\n53: \\n54:   > Note: The service mesh is not an overlay network. It\\n55:   > simplifies and enhances how microservices in an application talk to each\\n56:   > other over the network provided by the underlying platform.\\n57: \\n58: * **Ztunnel** - A lightweight data plane proxy written in Rust,\\n59:     used in Ambient mesh mode to provide secure connectivity and observability for workloads without sidecar proxies.\\n60: \\n61: - **Istiod** - The Istio control plane. It provides service discovery, configuration and certificate management.\\n62: \\n63: ## Repositories\\n64: \\n65: The Istio project is divided across a few GitHub repositories:\\n66: \\n67: - [istio/api](https://github.com/istio/api). This repository defines\\n68: component-level APIs and common configuration formats for the Istio platform.\\n69: \\n70: - [istio/community](https://github.com/istio/community). This repository contains\\n71: information on the Istio community, including the various documents that govern\\n72: the Istio open source project.\\n73: \\n74: - [istio/istio](README.md). This is the main code repository. It hosts Istio's\\n75: core components, install artifacts, and sample programs. It includes:\\n76: \\n77:     - [istioctl](istioctl/). This directory contains code for the\\n78: [_istioctl_](https://istio.io/latest/docs/reference/commands/istioctl/) command line utility.\\n79: \\n80:     - [pilot](pilot/). This directory\\n81: contains platform-specific code to populate the\\n82: [abstract service model](https://istio.io/docs/concepts/traffic-management/#pilot), dynamically reconfigure the proxies\\n83: when the application topology changes, as well as translate\\n84: [routing rules](https://istio.io/latest/docs/reference/config/networking/) into proxy specific configuration.\\n85: \\n86:     - [security](security/). This directory contains [security](https://istio.io/latest/docs/concepts/security/) related code.\\n87: \\n88: - [istio/proxy](https://github.com/istio/proxy). The Istio proxy contains\\n89: extensions to the [Envoy proxy](https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy) (in the form of\\n90: Envoy filters) that support authentication, authorization, and telemetry collection.\\n91: \\n92: - [istio/ztunnel](https://github.com/istio/ztunnel). The repository contains the Rust implementation of the ztunnel\\n93: component of Ambient mesh.\\n94: \\n95: - [istio/client-go](https://github.com/istio/client-go). This repository defines\\n96:   auto-generated Kubernetes clients for interacting with Istio resources programmatically.\\n97: \\n98: > [!NOTE]\\n99: > Only the `istio/api` and `istio/client-go` repositories expose stable interfaces intended for direct usage as libraries.\\n100: \\n101: ## Issue management\\n102: \\n103: We use GitHub to track all of our bugs and feature requests. Each issue we track has a variety of metadata:\\n104: \\n105: - **Epic**. An epic represents a feature area for Istio as a whole. Epics are fairly broad in scope and are basically product-level things.\\n106: Each issue is ultimately part of an epic.\\n107: \\n108: - **Milestone**. Each issue is assigned a milestone. This is 0.1, 0.2, ..., or 'Nebulous Future'. The milestone indicates when we\\n109: think the issue should get addressed.\\n110: \\n111: - **Priority**. Each issue has a priority which is represented by the column in the [Prioritization](https://github.com/orgs/istio/projects/6) project. Priority can be one of\\n112: P0, P1, P2, or >P2. The priority indicates how important it is to address the issue within the milestone. P0 says that the\\n113: milestone cannot be considered achieved if the issue isn't resolved.\\n114: \\n115: ---\\n116: \\n117: <div align=\\\"center\\\">\\n118:     <picture>\\n119:       <source media=\\\"(prefers-color-scheme: dark)\\\" srcset=\\\"https://raw.githubusercontent.com/cncf/artwork/refs/heads/main/other/cncf/horizontal/color-whitetext/cncf-color-whitetext.svg\\\">\\n120:       <source media=\\\"(prefers-color-scheme: light)\\\" srcset=\\\"https://raw.githubusercontent.com/cncf/artwork/master/other/cncf/horizontal/color/cncf-color.svg\\\">\\n121:       <img width=\\\"300\\\" alt=\\\"Cloud Native Computing Foundation logo\\\" src=\\\"https://raw.githubusercontent.com/cncf/artwork/refs/heads/main/other/cncf/horizontal/color-whitetext/cncf-color-whitetext.svg\\\">\\n122:     </picture>\\n123:     <p>Istio is a <a href=\\\"https://cncf.io\\\">Cloud Native Computing Foundation</a> project.</p>\\n124: </div>\\n125: \",\"url\":\"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/istio--f8af3cae@3a22a44f97d470ed898e4dfb3b17913cb295c7bf/-/blob/README.md\"}"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"a2b56f17-dd2d-42c6-a30e-fbb0c1207e35","uuid":"41591aec-aeca-4229-bf31-5846c66a4056","tool_use_result":{"content":"{\"content\":\"1: # Istio\n2: \n3: [![CII Best Practices](https://bestpractices.coreinfrastructure.org/projects/1395/badge)](https://bestpractices.coreinfrastructure.org/projects/1395)\n4: [![Go Report Card](https://goreportcard.com/badge/github.com/istio/istio)](https://goreportcard.com/report/github.com/istio/istio)\n5: [![GoDoc](https://godoc.org/istio.io/istio?status.svg)](https://godoc.org/istio.io/istio)\n6: \n7: <a href=\"https://istio.io/\">\n8:     <picture>\n9:       <source media=\"(prefers-color-scheme: dark)\" srcset=\"https://raw.githubusercontent.com/cncf/artwork/refs/heads/main/projects/istio/icon/color/istio-icon-color.svg\">\n10:       <source media=\"(prefers-color-scheme: light)\" srcset=\"https://github.com/istio/istio/raw/master/logo/istio-bluelogo-whitebackground-unframed.svg\">\n11:       <img title=\"Istio\" height=\"100\" width=\"100\" alt=\"Istio logo\" src=\"https://github.com/istio/istio/raw/master/logo/istio-bluelogo-whitebackground-unframed.svg\">\n12:     </picture>\n13: </a>\n14: \n15: ---\n16: \n17: Istio is an open source service mesh that layers transparently onto existing distributed applications. Istio’s powerful features provide a uniform and more efficient way to secure, connect, and monitor services. Istio is the path to load balancing, service-to-service authentication, and monitoring – with few or no service code changes.\n18: \n19: - For in-depth information about how to use Istio, visit [istio.io](https://istio.io)\n20: - To ask questions and get assistance from our community, visit [GitHub Discussions](https://github.com/istio/istio/discussions)\n21: - To learn how to participate in our overall community, visit [our community page](https://istio.io/about/community)\n22: \n23: In this README:\n24: \n25: - [Introduction](#introduction)\n26: - [Repositories](#repositories)\n27: - [Issue management](#issue-management)\n28: \n29: In addition, here are some other documents you may wish to read:\n30: \n31: - [Istio Community](https://github.com/istio/community#istio-community) - describes how to get involved and contribute to the Istio project\n32: - [Istio Developer's Guide](https://github.com/istio/istio/wiki/Preparing-for-Development) - explains how to set up and use an Istio development environment\n33: - [Project Conventions](https://github.com/istio/istio/wiki/Development-Conventions) - describes the conventions we use within the code base\n34: - [Creating Fast and Lean Code](https://github.com/istio/istio/wiki/Writing-Fast-and-Lean-Code) - performance-oriented advice and guidelines for the code base\n35: \n36: You'll find many other useful documents on our [Wiki](https://github.com/istio/istio/wiki).\n37: \n38: ## Introduction\n39: \n40: [Istio](https://istio.io/latest/docs/concepts/what-is-istio/) is an open platform for providing a uniform way to [integrate\n41: microservices](https://istio.io/latest/docs/examples/microservices-istio/), manage [traffic flow](https://istio.io/latest/docs/concepts/traffic-management/) across microservices, enforce policies\n42: and aggregate telemetry data. Istio's control plane provides an abstraction\n43: layer over the underlying cluster management platform, such as Kubernetes.\n44: \n45: Istio is composed of these components:\n46: \n47: - **Envoy** - Sidecar proxies per microservice to handle ingress/egress traffic\n48:    between services in the cluster and from a service to external\n49:    services. The proxies form a _secure microservice mesh_ providing a rich\n50:    set of functions like discovery, rich layer-7 routing, circuit breakers,\n51:    policy enforcement and telemetry recording/reporting\n52:    functions.\n53: \n54:   > Note: The service mesh is not an overlay network. It\n55:   > simplifies and enhances how microservices in an application talk to each\n56:   > other over the network provided by the underlying platform.\n57: \n58: * **Ztunnel** - A lightweight data plane proxy written in Rust,\n59:     used in Ambient mesh mode to provide secure connectivity and observability for workloads without sidecar proxies.\n60: \n61: - **Istiod** - The Istio control plane. It provides service discovery, configuration and certificate management.\n62: \n63: ## Repositories\n64: \n65: The Istio project is divided across a few GitHub repositories:\n66: \n67: - [istio/api](https://github.com/istio/api). This repository defines\n68: component-level APIs and common configuration formats for the Istio platform.\n69: \n70: - [istio/community](https://github.com/istio/community). This repository contains\n71: information on the Istio community, including the various documents that govern\n72: the Istio open source project.\n73: \n74: - [istio/istio](README.md). This is the main code repository. It hosts Istio's\n75: core components, install artifacts, and sample programs. It includes:\n76: \n77:     - [istioctl](istioctl/). This directory contains code for the\n78: [_istioctl_](https://istio.io/latest/docs/reference/commands/istioctl/) command line utility.\n79: \n80:     - [pilot](pilot/). This directory\n81: contains platform-specific code to populate the\n82: [abstract service model](https://istio.io/docs/concepts/traffic-management/#pilot), dynamically reconfigure the proxies\n83: when the application topology changes, as well as translate\n84: [routing rules](https://istio.io/latest/docs/reference/config/networking/) into proxy specific configuration.\n85: \n86:     - [security](security/). This directory contains [security](https://istio.io/latest/docs/concepts/security/) related code.\n87: \n88: - [istio/proxy](https://github.com/istio/proxy). The Istio proxy contains\n89: extensions to the [Envoy proxy](https://github.com/envoyproxy/envoy) (in the form of\n90: Envoy filters) that support authentication, authorization, and telemetry collection.\n91: \n92: - [istio/ztunnel](https://github.com/istio/ztunnel). The repository contains the Rust implementation of the ztunnel\n93: component of Ambient mesh.\n94: \n95: - [istio/client-go](https://github.com/istio/client-go). This repository defines\n96:   auto-generated Kubernetes clients for interacting with Istio resources programmatically.\n97: \n98: > [!NOTE]\n99: > Only the `istio/api` and `istio/client-go` repositories expose stable interfaces intended for direct usage as libraries.\n100: \n101: ## Issue management\n102: \n103: We use GitHub to track all of our bugs and feature requests. Each issue we track has a variety of metadata:\n104: \n105: - **Epic**. An epic represents a feature area for Istio as a whole. Epics are fairly broad in scope and are basically product-level things.\n106: Each issue is ultimately part of an epic.\n107: \n108: - **Milestone**. Each issue is assigned a milestone. This is 0.1, 0.2, ..., or 'Nebulous Future'. The milestone indicates when we\n109: think the issue should get addressed.\n110: \n111: - **Priority**. Each issue has a priority which is represented by the column in the [Prioritization](https://github.com/orgs/istio/projects/6) project. Priority can be one of\n112: P0, P1, P2, or >P2. The priority indicates how important it is to address the issue within the milestone. P0 says that the\n113: milestone cannot be considered achieved if the issue isn't resolved.\n114: \n115: ---\n116: \n117: <div align=\"center\">\n118:     <picture>\n119:       <source media=\"(prefers-color-scheme: dark)\" srcset=\"https://raw.githubusercontent.com/cncf/artwork/refs/heads/main/other/cncf/horizontal/color-whitetext/cncf-color-whitetext.svg\">\n120:       <source media=\"(prefers-color-scheme: light)\" srcset=\"https://raw.githubusercontent.com/cncf/artwork/master/other/cncf/horizontal/color/cncf-color.svg\">\n121:       <img width=\"300\" alt=\"Cloud Native Computing Foundation logo\" src=\"https://raw.githubusercontent.com/cncf/artwork/refs/heads/main/other/cncf/horizontal/color-whitetext/cncf-color-whitetext.svg\">\n122:     </picture>\n123:     <p>Istio is a <a href=\"https://cncf.io\">Cloud Native Computing Foundation</a> project.</p>\n124: </div>\n125: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/istio--f8af3cae@3a22a44f97d470ed898e4dfb3b17913cb295c7bf/-/blob/README.md"}}}
